Architecture: **4-tier memory consolidation** (Working→Episodic→Semantic→Procedural, Ebbinghaus decay) + **triple-stream RRF search** (BM25+Vector+Graph) + **12 auto-capture hooks** + 51 MCP tools + 107 REST endpoints + 15+ agent platforms. **PRIMARY: NEW Pattern #85 Platform-Primitive Foundation N=1 stale-flagged** — corpus-first: built ENTIRELY on iii-engine's primitives, self-identifies as *"a running iii instance,"* delegates ALL infrastructure, counts in host units, extends via host CLI; 4 promotion criteria; coupling-risk built into definition; full proposal-document at `03 Projects/agentmemory - Beginner Analysis/01 Analysis/(C) Pattern Platform-Primitive Foundation N=1 registration proposal.md`. **NEW Pattern #18 sub-archetype: shared-backend-service** (one server, 15+ platforms as clients — 3rd multi-platform mechanism after Layer 1 coexistence + Layer 2 translation). **NEW observational candidate: AI-Generated-Repo Artifact Contamination** (DESIGN.md ships 288 lines of unrelated "Lamborghini design system" boilerplate — verified 3 ways: 2 WebFetch + raw curl — corpus-first provably-contaminated governance file; bundled with viral-velocity-outpacing-quality-maturity observation; counter-evidence vs Pattern #12 file-count proxy). **6 within-pattern strengthenings**: Pattern #8 first memory-retrieval-domain benchmark (LongMemEval-S ICLR 2025, 95.2% R@5) + Pattern #28 STRONG dual-axis multi-provider (LLM + embeddings) + Pattern #12 counter-evidence + Pattern #81 "names-the-drift-and-drifts-anyway" + Pattern #83 MIXED partial evidence (**NOT a clean N=3** — README over-claims while CHANGELOG/ROADMAP honest) + Pattern #19/#57. **Pattern #52 OBSERVATIONAL watch** (v69 sustained-velocity re-check). **Storm Bear meta-entity Phase 0.9 4-of-4 STRICT PASS → STRONG INCLUDE** — FIRST 4/4 in the post-amendment window; streak → 2; 10-instance window v57-v66 = 80% INCLUDE. **Highest-relevance pilot candidate in recent corpus** — persistent memory for the vault's own Claude Code substrate; recommended as a FENCED pilot (scratch project → read-mostly vault → decision gate), NOT a substrate swap; the vault has already hit the failure mode agentmemory targets (584 KB CLAUDE.md refactor). **7 corpus-firsts.** Sibling to vault project graphify (knowledge-graph search stream). State: 26 → **27 active** / 0.605 → **0.628 ratio**; **v68 stale-checks: Pattern #85 + Pattern #18 shared-backend-service sub-archetype**; v68/v69 AI-Generated-Repo Contamination observational; v69 Pattern #52 sustained-velocity. ⚠️ Build note: `DESIGN.md` content-contamination is a real repo artifact, NOT a fetch error — excluded as a source per "NEVER fabricate" discipline.

**v116 Sana** (2026-05-29): **⚠️ OPERATOR OVERRIDE — STRICT Phase 0.9 verdict = 0/4 SKIP; force-built by operator decision = 2nd operator-elected override in corpus history (after v84 image-blaster). First wiki under routine v2.4.** `NVlabs/Sana` = "SANA: Efficient High-Resolution Image Synthesis with Linear Diffusion Transformer" — NVIDIA Labs' efficiency-first text-to-image (+ now text-to-video / world-model) generation framework. **NOT an agent, NOT a coding tool, NOT a Claude-Code skill, NO SKILL.md/AGENTS.md/.claude/, NOT in the agentskills.io ecosystem.** **Author NVIDIA Labs** (`owner.type: Organization`) = research division of NVIDIA Corp (US mega-corp); algorithm credit shared with **MIT Han Lab (Song Han)** + **Tsinghua**. **7,919 stars / 607 forks / 95 subscribers / 123 open issues / created 2024-10-11 / pushed 2026-05-28 (~595 days / ~1.6 yr) = ~13.3 stars/day SUSTAINED-LOW = NOT a Pattern #52 instance** (below all sub-class floors; profile like v100 Easydict ~10.3/d — a long-lived steady-accrual repo, not a viral pulse); fork_ratio 607/7,919 = **0.077**; **Apache-2.0** (code; GitHub API agrees) with **model weights licensed separately per HF collection = a code-vs-weights license boundary**; **Python ~93.5%**; default branch `main`; homepage nvlabs.github.io/Sana/docs/; topics diffusion/dit/linear-transformer/nvfp4/pytorch/reinforcement-learning/text-to-image/text-to-video/video-generation/world-models. **Core architecture (genuinely instructive — in efficient generative vision, a DIFFERENT field)**: (1) **DC-AE Deep Compression Autoencoder 32×** (vs conventional 8× → ~16× fewer latent tokens = the main high-res-speed lever); (2) **Linear-attention DiT + Mix-FFN** (cost ~linear in token count, essential at 4K); (3) **decoder-only LLM (Gemma-family) text encoder** with in-context-learning prompting (the ONE thin thread to the LLM world the corpus tracks — but an internal component, not an agent surface); **v144 headroom** (2026-06-03) — **GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4** [routine v2.6 §31; (a) **FAIL** undisclosed individual / not (a)-7 + (b) **STRONG** (load-bearing) context-compression infrastructure for AI coding agents + the most directly-vault-applicable subject in a long run + (c) STRONG multi-mechanism engine + (d) STRONG token-compression cluster + MCP + context-rot corpus-recursive]. `chopratejas/headroom` = **"Headroom compresses everything your AI agent reads — tool outputs, logs, RAG chunks, files, and conversation history — before it reaches the LLM. Same answers, fraction of the tokens."** Tagline *"The context compression layer for AI agents."* By **chopratejas** (likely Tejas Chopra, Indian-heritage name; no name/role/location disclosed in-repo — confidence speculation). A context layer sitting **between an AI coding agent and the LLM** (Claude Code / Cursor / Codex / Aider / multi-agent), shrinking the agent's read-context with **content-aware compressors (NOT LLM-summarization):** SmartCrusher (universal JSON) + CodeCompressor (AST-aware Python/JS/Go/Rust/Java/C++) + **Kompress-base** ("our HuggingFace model trained on agentic traces", prose) + CacheAligner (stabilizes prefixes for provider KV-cache hits) + **CCR reversible compression** (originals kept locally, LLM fetches via `headroom_retrieve` — "originals never deleted"). Repo-stated benchmarks: code-search 17,765→1,408 (92%), SRE 65,694→5,118 (92%), GitHub triage 54,174→14,761 (73%); accuracy preserved (GSM8K 0.870→0.870, TruthfulQA +0.030, SQuAD-v2 97% @ 19%). **Five deployment surfaces:** Python lib (`pip install "headroom-ai[all]"`) / TS lib (`npm install headroom-ai`) / HTTP proxy (`headroom proxy --port 8787`, zero code change) / CLI wrapper (`headroom wrap claude|aider|copilot`) / MCP server (`headroom mcp install`); Docker `ghcr.io/chopratejas/headroom`; Python 3.10+. **MCP tools:** `headroom_compress` / `headroom_retrieve` / `headroom_stats`. **Plus** `headroom learn` (failure-mining: mines failed agent sessions → auto-writes corrections to `CLAUDE.md`/`AGENTS.md`/`GEMINI.md`; plugin-based for Claude/Codex/Gemini) + **SharedContext** (compressed context passing across multi-agent workflows: shared store + agent provenance + auto-dedup). Works with **13 agents** (Claude Code + Codex + Gemini CLI + Hermes Agent + Qwen Code + Kimi CLI + OpenClaw + OpenCode + Cursor + Qoder + CodeBuddy + WorkBuddy + GitHub Copilot) via **managed hook files** (Claude-style JSON installed into `~/.claude/settings.json`, `~/.qwen/settings.json`, a Hermes plugin `~/.hermes/plugins/ping_island/`, OpenClaw gateway hooks) + live **`codex app-server` WebSocket** + **SSH tunnel forwarding** of remote sessions (bootstraps a `PingIslandBridge` onto remote hosts, rewrites their hooks to target it — "SSH support is a core workflow, not a sidecar script") + IDE extensions + multi-client transcript backfill (reads `~/.openclaw/agents/main/sessions/` for full context). Cosmetic layer: per-client animated mascots + sound packs (OpenPeon/CESP + 8-bit). Explicitly framed (verbatim): treats agent approvals + input requests as **"actionable focus interrupts"** routed back to the source, *"rather than read-only dashboards."* Owner `erha19` (no name/affiliation/location disclosed in the repo); v0.21.1; 832★. **v162 agent-of-empires ship 2026-06-15 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 [(a) FAIL · (b) STRONG · (c) STRONG · (d) STRONG]; 10th consecutive goal-aligned ship (v153→v162); §35 stays clear (0 OG in window); PRIMARY = the genuine 2nd "session-hosting multiplexer for AI coding agents" instance → species N=2 (DECOMPOSES the v151/v158 held-heterogeneous orchestration theme; confirm/rename DEFERRED to the audit); 0 new §C standalones. ⚠️ Shipped as v162 NOT v161 — v161 was already CodePilot; the root shim was stale at v160 (never recorded CodePilot) → brought current + drift flagged this ship. SHIPS INTO the v158-audit-CONFIRMED Pattern Library.** `agent-of-empires/agent-of-empires` (AoE; canonical owner-fork `njbrake/agent-of-empires`) = *"A session manager for AI coding agents on Linux and macOS. Use it from the terminal (TUI) or from any browser (web dashboard). Run multiple AI agents in parallel across different branches of your codebase, each in its own isolated session with optional Docker sandboxing."* A **human-driven multiplexer** (Rust 68.7% + TypeScript 29.7%; MIT; Linux+macOS) that runs multiple AI coding agents **in parallel** — each in its own persistent **tmux** session on an auto-created **git worktree** (branch isolation without manual branch-management), optionally inside a **Docker / Podman / Apple-Container sandbox** with configurable host-dir mounts; sessions survive TUI-close / SSH-disconnect / reboot. Two front-ends: a ratatui **TUI** (`cargo build`) and an opt-in React 19 / Vite / Tailwind v4 / xterm.js **web dashboard / PWA** (`cargo build --features serve`). An **Agent Client Protocol (ACP) "structured view"** (plan panels / tool-call cards / **swipe-to-approve**, mobile-first; raw-tmux passthrough as the universal fallback) via a top-level `acp-worker/`. **`R`-to-expose-the-dashboard-over-HTTPS** for phone access (Tailscale Funnel / Cloudflare Tunnel + QR + passphrase). **CLI + HTTP API** to drive sessions from external orchestrators (*"integrates with tools like OpenClaw"*). Multi-repo workspaces, diff viewing, file editing, status detection, sound/push notifications, Nix flake. Distinctive engineering: a single-source-of-truth config via a **`#[setting(...)]` Rust attribute macro** (one field auto-generates the TUI + web + server surfaces via schema derivation) + server-projected theming (`Theme` → `ResolvedTheme`); a `DESIGN.md` aesthetic design-language doc ("Industrial Warmth," anti-"Linear-style-template," benchmarked vs Warp/Zed/Ghostty; namesake "Empire" theme = the Age-of-Empires pun is intentional); heavy CI (Codecov 75%-patch gate + no-regression, dual Playwright suites + coverage-matrix.json, git-cliff changelog, weekly automated staging-PR releases). Supports **13 auto-detected agents** (Claude Code + OpenCode + Mistral Vibe + Codex + Gemini + Antigravity + Cursor + Copilot + Pi.dev + Factory Droid + Hermes + Kiro + Qwen). By **Nate (Nathan) Brake** (`njbrake` / @natebrake), ML Engineer at **Mozilla.ai**; *"Maintained by the Agent of Empires community, with support from Mozilla.ai"* (org/owner split: `njbrake/agent-of-empires` person-fork vs `agent-of-empires/agent-of-empires` community org — same codebase, two front doors). v1.11.0; ≈2.6k★. ## v163 — ai-maestro (23blocks-OS / Juan Pelaez) — 2026-06-15 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4

**`23blocks-OS/ai-maestro` ("AI Maestro")** = *"AI Agent Orchestrator with Skills System — Give AI Agents superpowers: memory search, code graph queries, agent-to-agent messaging. Manage Claude, Codex or any AI Agent from one dashboard. Move Agents between computers and locations."* Tagline: *"The OS for AI-first organizations — orchestrate any AI agent with persistent memory, agent-to-agent messaging, and multi-machine support."* README origin: *"I was running 35 AI agents across multiple terminals and became the human mailman between them. So I built AI Maestro."* A **self-hosted multi-vendor orchestration PLATFORM** (TypeScript 87.8% + Shell 6.6% + JS + HCL; MIT) that manages **Claude Code / Codex / Aider / Cursor / OpenClaw / Hermes / Droid** (or any terminal agent, "we don't lock you in") from one **Next.js + xterm.js + Tailwind dashboard**; gives agents **persistent memory** (CozoDB semantic store) + an interactive **code graph** (ts-morph + delta indexing) + **agent-to-agent messaging**; runs them across a **multi-machine peer mesh** (every machine equal, auto-discover, no central server) in **four deploy modes** (local tmux / Docker / AWS EC2 ARM64+Nginx+SSL / AWS ECS Fargate, Terraform-provisioned). Three home-grown **open protocols**: **AMP** (Agent Messaging Protocol — email-like agent-to-agent messaging with cryptographic signatures + cross-machine push; the product's reason to exist) · **AID** (Agent Identity — portable cryptographic identity) · **AAP** (Agent Actions Protocol — standardized tool/API/workflow execution). Ships a **Claude Code plugin (5 skills + 32 CLI scripts)** + a Plugin Builder (`23blocks-OS/ai-maestro-plugins`) + the **LolaBot** open-source "Chief of Staff" agent template (`23blocks-OS/lolabot`); gateway integrations Slack/Discord/Email/WhatsApp; security-forward (crypto-signed messages + a content gateway screening **34 prompt-injection patterns**). By **Juan Pelaez** (`@jkpelaez` / `jpelaez-23blocks`), CTO & Founder of **3Metas + 23blocks** (Boulder USA / Roma Italy); site ai-maestro.23blocks.com; `curl -fsSL …/remote-install.sh | sh`. v0.35.54; ≈713★.

**(a) FAIL** — Juan Pelaez = a named **US/Italy founder** (CTO & Founder, 3Metas + 23blocks); not a VN/Asian-cluster cultural-peer, not (a)-7 (23blocks is not a vault-substrate dependency the vault runs on — Anthropic-tier); notable-founder ≠ (a) PASS (the v139/v159-steipete discipline); **no axis minted.** **(b) STRONG (not STRONGEST)** — orchestrates multiple heterogeneous coding agents as units (dashboard + AMP messaging + memory + code-graph + mesh + Claude Code plugin) = dead-center goal #1 + close to Storm Bear's own workflow (the "human mailman" pain = running many parallel Claude Code agents); **STRONG-not-STRONGEST** = a third-party orchestration control-plane *around* the agents (the Paseo/cmux/AoE/ai-switcher calibration; STRONGEST reserved for the substrate Claude/Anthropic or a methodology v126). **(c) STRONG** — mature TS+infra (995 commits / v0.35.54; CozoDB + ts-morph + delta-indexing + 4 deploy modes + Terraform + Vitest; AMP/AID/AAP protocols; multi-machine peer mesh; crypto-signatures + 34-injection-pattern content gateway). **(d) STRONG** — orchestration-PLATFORM standalone N=2 with Paseo + completes the 2nd bucket of the v162 decomposition + #84 7-agent cross-tool + OpenClaw/Hermes corpus-recursive + memory↔v66/v132 & code-graph↔v70 absorption + T4c gateways + #66 supply-chain + #57 5-skill Claude Code plugin.

## v165 — lazyagent (illegalstudio / nahime0) — 2026-06-15 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 — clean observability instance + 1 corpus-first capability mint

**`illegalstudio/lazyagent`** = *"Monitor all your coding agents from one terminal — Claude Code, Cursor, OpenCode, pi and more."* / *"A terminal UI, macOS menu bar app, and HTTP API for monitoring all your coding agents from a single place."* A **multi-interface monitoring tool** whose thesis is *observe, don't replace*: **"lazyagent doesn't replace your workflow — it watches it. Launch agents wherever you want (terminal, IDE, desktop app), lazyagent just observes."** No server, no account, no lock-in; purely local + observational (reads each agent's local session data). **Four delivery surfaces:** a lazygit-style **Terminal UI** (inspect projects/sessions/agents/subagents/tools/prompts/outputs in one view) + a **macOS menu-bar app** (Wails GUI) + a **Bearer-token HTTP API** (build your own clients) + a **paid iOS App Store companion** (pairs with the API; funds dev). Tracks in real time: activity, **per-session token breakdowns** (model / cache-reuse-saved / cache-creation) and **cost**. **9 agents:** Claude Code · Cursor · Codex · Grok CLI · Kilo · Kimi Code CLI · Amp · pi · OpenCode. **Distinctive — maintenance commands over stored transcripts:** `prune` (delete chats older than N days; dry-run + auto-backup) · `compact` (shrink session files by truncating bulk payloads; ~80+ MiB/yr) · `search` (full-text transcript search w/ snippets) · `limits` (rate-limit/billing summaries). Self-credited lineage: lazygit / lazyworktree / pixel-agents. Owner org `illegalstudio`, handle `nahime0` (X @nahime0); Go 91.3% (+ TS 4.5% / Svelte 3.8%); MIT; v0.12.5; ≈165★. ⚠️ **Name collision:** `chojs23/lazyagent` (v0.3.1) is a *different* similarly-named project — the canonical subject is `illegalstudio/lazyagent` per the operator URL (the v148 cataloguing-hazard lesson).

"illegalstudio" = a brand, not a geo/cultural signal. ## v166 ai-agent-session-center ship 2026-06-15 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 [(a) FAIL · (b) STRONG · (c) STRONG · (d) STRONG]; 14th consecutive goal-aligned ship (v153→v166); §35 stays clear (window {v164 GA, v165 GA, v166 GA} = 0 OG)

`coding-by-feng/ai-agent-session-center` = *"Real-time dashboard that turns AI coding agent sessions (Claude Code, Gemini CLI, Codex) into animated 3D robots — with live terminals, prompt history, tool logs, and queuing. Runs on any device."* A self-hosted **web dashboard** (`npx ai-agent-session-center` → `localhost:3333`) that **OBSERVES** multiple AI-coding-agent sessions and renders each as an animated 3D robot (6 procedural models robot/mech/drone/spider/orb/tank; **8 run-state animation states** idle/walk/run/wait/dance/wave/offline driven by Idle/Prompting/Working/Waiting/Approval/Input/Ended), alongside live terminals (xterm.js), prompt history, and tool logs. Node 18+/Express 5 + `ws` + `node-pty` backend; React 19/TypeScript/Vite + **Three.js/React-Three-Fiber** frontend; SQLite-WAL (server) + IndexedDB (browser); 400+ Vitest tests + Playwright E2E. MIT; TypeScript 81.4%; ≈72★/9 forks/200 commits/v2.10.30 (Jun 7 2026, "appears to be a test/CI date"). Owner `coding-by-feng` (no disclosed name/affiliation/location).

**The load-bearing architectural fact (verified this ship): OBSERVES, does not host.** README: *"No modifications to any CLI are needed. The hooks are purely observational."* Integration = `npm run install-hooks` writes lightweight bash hooks into the CLIs' configs; hooks append JSON events to `/tmp/claude-session-center/queue.jsonl`; the Node server watches that file + broadcasts over WebSocket. **The user launches Claude Code/Gemini/Codex independently; the dashboard discovers them via hooks, it does not spawn/own the agent processes** (contrast v99 cmux / v162 AoE which host the sessions in PTYs/tmux they own). The `node-pty`/`xterm.js` "live terminals" attach/display; they are not how the agents are launched. → **NOT the session-hosting-multiplexer species** (that species stays N=2 = cmux + AoE; the wrinkle flagged at intake is resolved against multiplexer).

**PRIMARY = a CLEAN instance-strengthening (the v164/v165 shape — 0 mints)** → the v158-CONFIRMED **"AI-Agent Observability / Status-Surface Tool" sub-archetype N=11 → N=12.** **0 new §C standalones; 46 patterns / 10 Library-vocab CONFIRMED UNCHANGED.** (a) **FAIL** [bare handle `coding-by-feng`; "feng" = a Chinese-surname *heritage hint*, not a disclosed identity → no cultural-peer inferred, the v139/v160/v164/v165 discipline + v151-audit rec (ii) "require a *solid* (a) signal, not a name/heritage inference"; no axis minted] · (b) **STRONG-not-STRONGEST** [monitoring Claude Code + Gemini + Codex = goal #1 + a real heavy-Claude-Code vault workflow, but an observability surface *around* the agents — the v154/v158/v164/v165 calibration] · (c) **STRONG** [Node/Express + React 19/Three.js + xterm/node-pty + SQLite-WAL; 400+ Vitest + Playwright E2E; 200 commits; mature for 72★] · (d) **STRONG** [observability sub-archetype + #84 cross-tool (3 agents + OpenCode/Cursor/Windsurf compat) + hooks-integration mechanism shared w/ v156/v160/v164 + Three.js/web-dashboard form].

**Why 0 mints (the v159/v164/v165 anti-inflation discipline):** its distinctive features are **blend + delivery, not structure** — it blends sub-flavor **(b) ambient/affective** (3D robots react to run-state = the web-dashboard cousin of the v154/v155/v156/v164 desktop-pets) with **(c) attention/approval-routing** (approve/deny tool requests, Approval/Input states, Alert = the v160 ping-island idea, here a minor feature) plus a **light prompt-queue orchestration** layer (global queue + auto-send-when-idle), all delivered as a **web 3D dashboard.** Multi-sub-flavor blend + novel UI form factor = scale/delivery (the v164 pet+metering-blend / v159 broadest-coverage line); a 4th "dashboard/mission-control" sub-flavor would inflate (the v160/v165 discipline). **Boundary lines:** **NOT session-multiplexer** (observes-not-hosts, see above) · **NOT LV-C7 #22** (observes + light prompt-queue + approve/deny *pass-through of the agents' own prompts* + kill/archive/delete *sessions* ≠ provider/account/config control; the prompt-queue auto-send = orchestration-lite OBSERVATION, the v156 permission-bubble precedent) · **NOT #18 #8** (no provider aggregation/routing) · **NOT a new sub-flavor.** Observations (NOT minted): hooks-event-file `/tmp/...queue.jsonl` mechanism (cousin of JSONL-parsing v89/v158 but event-emitting hooks, not reading the agents' own session JSONL) · 3D-robot/Three.js ambient viz = novel *delivery* of the ambient/affective idea (web vs desktop-pet) · **prompt-queue + auto-send-when-idle = orchestration-lite WATCH** (a 2nd "observe + queue/dispatch prompts to idle sessions" subject could justify a sub-flavor — not before) · #84 cross-tool (3 agents + compat).

## v168 — ponytail (DietrichGebert) — 2026-06-20 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 — ✅ VARIES THE DOMAIN (1st non-operating-niche ship since the v153→v166 run); 1 NEW §C standalone + clean #84 84c strengthening

**`DietrichGebert/ponytail`** = *"He says nothing. He writes one line. It works."* / *"Makes your AI agent think like the laziest senior dev in the room. The best code is the code you never wrote."* A **cross-harness ruleset-plugin** that makes AI coding agents write *minimal, necessary* code by injecting a **decision-ladder** into the agent's pre-generation planning — **NOT** a tool that operates/monitors/hosts agents (the v153→v166 niche); it changes **what the agent writes.** Decision-ladder (verbatim `AGENTS.md`): (1) *"Does this need to be built at all? (YAGNI)"* (2) stdlib? use it (3) native platform feature? use it (4) installed dependency? use it (5) *"Can this be one line? Make it one line."* (6) *"Only then: write the minimum code that works."* Explicit **NOT-lazy carve-outs** (the safety spine): input-validation-at-trust-boundaries / error-handling-preventing-data-loss / security / accessibility / hardware-calibration; non-trivial logic needs *"ONE runnable check behind."* Installs as a **Claude Code plugin** (`/plugin marketplace add DietrichGebert/ponytail`), a Codex/Copilot-CLI plugin, an **MCP server** (`ponytail-mcp/`), or by copying native rule files. **14 declared platforms** (Claude Code + Codex + Copilot CLI + Cursor + Windsurf + Cline + OpenCode + Gemini/Antigravity CLI + OpenClaw + Kiro + Aider + Zed + CodeWhale + Pi). **Mode levels** lite/full(default)/ultra/off (`/ponytail [mode]` or `PONYTAIL_DEFAULT_MODE`; runtime hook writes `.ponytail-active`). **Slash commands:** `/ponytail-review` (diff delete-list, tags delete/stdlib/native/yagni/shrink) · `/ponytail-audit` (whole-repo) · `/ponytail-debt` (harvest `ponytail:` markers into a debt ledger) · `/ponytail-gain` (scoreboard — **explicitly FORBIDS per-repo savings claims**) · `/ponytail-help`. **Rigorous DUAL benchmark** (`benchmarks/`): single-shot (80–94% fewer lines, but authors **self-flag as a "conversational artifact" / un-defensible**) + **agentic primary** (n=4, **Haiku 4.5**, `tiangolo/full-stack-fastapi-template`, 12 feature + 6 safety tasks, **3 arms** baseline/`caveman`-control/ponytail, git-diff + API telemetry + **secondary Sonnet-4.6 LLM judge**): **−54% lines / −22% tokens / −20% cost / −27% time / 100% safety** (YAGNI-variant 95%, failing a path-traversal guard = the safety↔minimalism trade-off shown honestly). ## v169 — SkillSpector (NVIDIA) — 2026-06-20 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 — CORPUS-FIRST defensive-security scanner for the agent-skills ecosystem + FIRST NVIDIA-org author; 1 NEW §C standalone (NO count change)

**`NVIDIA/SkillSpector`** = *"Security scanner for AI agent skills. Detect vulnerabilities, malicious patterns, and security risks."* A **defensive-security scanner** that analyzes an AI-agent *skill package* **before install** (point it at a dir or git URL) and returns a **risk score 0–100** + severity + recommendations. Targets the skill/extension artifacts of **Claude Code / Codex CLI / Gemini CLI / MCP**. **TWO-STAGE pipeline:** fast **static** pass (pattern-match + Python **AST** + **taint-tracking** + **YARA** signatures) → **optional LLM semantic** pass (reasons about intent, cuts false-positives; `--no-llm` runs static-only, free). **64 vulnerability patterns / 16 categories** (prompt-injection, data-exfiltration, privilege-escalation, supply-chain, dangerous code-exec). **MCP-specific:** tool-poisoning + least-privilege/permission-declaration-mismatch detection. **Live CVE (SC4):** queries **OSV.dev** in real-time w/ automatic offline fallback, no auth. **Multi-format output:** terminal/json/markdown/**SARIF** (CI + IDE security panels). **Pluggable multi-LLM-provider backend** (OpenAI / Anthropic / NVIDIA `build.nvidia.com` via `SKILLSPECTOR_PROVIDER`; Claude-Opus Anthropic default per `model_registry.yaml`). **Exportable LangGraph workflow** (Python API). Install: clone + `uv venv` + `make install`, OR Docker (`make docker-build` → `docker run … skillspector scan ./my-skill/ --no-llm`). **Apache-2.0; Python 96.8% + YARA 2.1%.** Owner = **`NVIDIA` org** — the **FIRST NVIDIA-authored subject in the 169-wiki corpus** (v72 referenced NVIDIA NIM as a *provider* only). Research-grounded design rationale: a README-cited study *"Agent Skills in the Wild"* (Liu et al., 2026; 42,447 skills; 26.1% vulnerable / 5.2% likely-malicious / scripts 2.12× more vulnerable) — **page-stated, third-party, unlinked, unverified** (see §37).

STRONG-not-STRONGEST = a 3rd-party tool *about* skills (passive validation), not the substrate or a behavior layer. **(c) STRONG** — mature LangGraph 2-stage pipeline + 16-category YARA + AST + taint-tracking + live OSV.dev + MCP-aware + SARIF/CI + Docker/pre-commit/model-registry; Apache-2.0. ## v171 — devspace (Waishnav) — 2026-06-20 — GOAL-ALIGNED INCLUDE 3/4 — CORPUS-FIRST self-hosted MCP bridge that turns a hosted chat host into a local coding agent; 1 NEW §C standalone + clean Pattern #18 B1-MCP strengthening (NO count change)

**`Waishnav/devspace`** = tagline *"Turn ChatGPT into Codex"* / *"Bring a Codex-style coding workflow to ChatGPT."* A **self-hosted MCP server** that gives a *hosted chat host* (ChatGPT first; "and Claude" / any MCP-capable host) the ability to **read / write / edit / search / execute code in local projects** — *without uploading files.* You install it on your own machine; the host connects over a local endpoint (`127.0.0.1:7676/mcp`) or a public HTTPS tunnel and behaves like a full local coding agent. **Tool surface:** read/write/edit files · search code + inspect dirs · run shell (tests/builds/git/package scripts) · **git-worktree isolation for parallel coding sessions** · follow **`AGENTS.md` + `CLAUDE.md`** · **discover local agent skills from skill folders** (`SKILL.md`) · tool cards + change summaries. **Security model (the load-bearing part of a remote→local bridge):** owner-password approval page at connect (password printed by `devspace init`, stored `~/.devspace/auth.json`) + folder-root allowlist ("you decide which roots are allowed") + explicit "treat a connected client like a **trusted coding partner with access to your machine**" disclosure. **Stack:** TypeScript 87.3% / JS 8.2% / CSS 4.3%; Node ≥20.12 <27 (22 LTS rec); Vite; npm `@waishnav/devspace` → `devspace init` → `devspace serve`. Author **Waishnav** (@wshxnv), GitCMS creator, *"on a journey to build a single-person company doing multiple millions in revenue"*; thesis *"My bet is that ChatGPT becomes the operating system for everything."* **Returns to the goal-#1 substrate core (MCP infra for coding agents)** after 3 domain-varying ships (v168/v169/v170) — a fresh shape, NOT the v153→v166 operating/monitoring niche.
